msg:HUALUXE Sanya is refreshed hotel after renovation (as far as I remember in 2023). And it's not just a word- that absolutale new one hotel.
The time of stay is April 2024. The stay was excellant. The hotel is located in a bay where there is no fuss and noise, great for families with children. The hotel has a large, well-maintained territory with green areas and recreation areas. As presented on the website, there are 2 large games rooms, one with access to the street, the staff is very friendly, socks are given out at the entrance to the children's area for the safety of your children, the girls working with children are very friendly to children and create a festive mood. Unfortunately children cars in a "Sun park" were broken during the stay- hope it will be repaired late.
There is a swimming pool with a children's water park where foam parties are held. Very cozy, clean, comfortable rooms. The hotel staff tries in every possible way to create exactly the feeling of relaxation and help you relax. Hotel provide Chinese-speaking  stuff and English-speaking stuff (from Nepal as far as I remember).
I would like to express my deep gratitude to Rosie, this is a person who will help not only solve issues related to the hotel, but also help deal with personal issues related to vacation at all and being in China in particular. As example Rosie helped with package delivery service not related to the hotel. Small amount of Chinese stuff speak english- Rosie speak.
I fully recommend this hotel for your confidant and comfortable stay.
